<div>   
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">       </span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">谨以此文，敬献西南科技大学70周年校庆。</span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><img title alt="1.jpg" src="https://cors.zfour.workers.dev/?http://image.sciencenet.cn/home/202206/29/165155d57ooltsov558iif.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">    </span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">       这近万平米水域，是挖掘早期一个足球场而建造的。武都引水工程的右岸水渠，从龙门山脉奔流而下，长驱五十公里后，在我们学校中央，巍峨龙山的东侧，形成一片宽阔湖面。</span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><img title alt="2.jpg" src="https://cors.zfour.workers.dev/?http://image.sciencenet.cn/home/202206/29/165047ossyhiyodssykkyd.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">    </span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">       这是校园风景的点睛之笔，自建成那天起，就波光粼粼，映出草木繁盛。无论昼夜晨昏，还是雨雪阴晴，显现出不同风姿，变换着瑰丽色彩。</span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"> </span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><img title alt="3.jpg" src="https://cors.zfour.workers.dev/?http://image.sciencenet.cn/home/202206/29/170244w3i7e4d2a100x4o4.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">    </span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">       <span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">春天，这里是殷红。低山上的梅，还在早春二月，就一个蓓蕾接着一个蓓蕾，从严寒中苏醒过来，像溅出的火星子，一点点、一团团，渐呈燎原之势。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><br></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: left;"><span font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;"><span style="font-family: 幼圆; font-size: 16px;">       不需半月光景，就从坡顶漫至山脚，自堤岸涌上小岛。恰好仲春三月，山茶花接着开了，开得风姿绰约。紫藤花接着开了，开得优雅淡定。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p style="text-align: 秋天，这里是明黄。新生入学的九、十月，湖边的山坡上，突然就开出了黄花槐，明亮朴素的颜色，投影在清澈湖水中，映射到寂寞蓝天上，像期待成熟的眼睛，历经坎坷后的平静。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p
